Hop = function() -- proto 210
   local r0_pr210 = game.PlaceId
   local r1_pr210 = {}
   local r2_pr210 = ""
   local r3_pr210 = os.date("!*t").hour
   local r4_pr210 = false
   TPReturner = function() -- proto 1
      local r0_pr210_1
      if r2_pr210 ~= "" then
         r0_pr210_1 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..r0_pr210.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor="..r2_pr210))
      else
         r0_pr210_1 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..r0_pr210.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"))
      end
      local r1_pr210_1 = ""
      if r0_pr210_1.nextPageCursor and r0_pr210_1.nextPageCursor ~= "null" and r0_pr210_1.nextPageCursor ~= "null" then
         r2_pr210 = r0_pr210_1.nextPageCursor
      end
      local r2_pr210_1 = 0
      for r6_pr210_1, r7_pr210_1 in pairs(r0_pr210_1.data) do
         -- backwards jump barrier
         local r8_pr210_1 = true
         r1_pr210_1 = tostring(r7_pr210_1.id)
         if tonumber(r7_pr210_1.maxPlayers) > tonumber(r7_pr210_1.playing) then
            for r12_pr210_1, r13_pr210_1 in pairs(r1_pr210) do
               -- backwards jump barrier
               if r2_pr210_1 ~= 0 then
                  if r1_pr210_1 == tostring(r13_pr210_1) then
                     r8_pr210_1 = false
                  end
               else
                  if tonumber(r3_pr210) ~= tonumber(r13_pr210_1) then
                     local r14_pr210_1 = pcall(function() -- proto 1
                        r1_pr210 = {}
                        table.insert(r1_pr210, r3_pr210)
                     end)
                  end
               end
               r2_pr210_1 = r2_pr210_1 + 1
            end
            if r8_pr210_1 == true then
               table.insert(r1_pr210, r1_pr210_1)
               wait(0.1)
               pcall(function() -- proto 0
                  wait()
                  game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(r0_pr210, r1_pr210_1, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
               end)
               wait(0.1)
            end
         end
      end
   end
   Teleport = function() -- proto 0
      -- backwards jump barrier
      while wait(0.1) do
         pcall(function() -- proto 0
            TPReturner()
            if r2_pr210 ~= "" then
               TPReturner()
            end
         end)
      end
   end
   Teleport()
end

LockTween = function() -- proto 30
   if _G.LockTween then
      return
   end

   wait()
   local r0_pr30 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
   if r0_pr30 and r0_pr30:IsDescendantOf(game.Workspace) then
      local r1_pr30 = r0_pr30:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
      if r1_pr30 then
         r1_pr30.CFrame = r1_pr30.CFrame
      end
   end
   wait()

      r0_pr30.BodyClip:Destroy()
   end
   if r0_pr30:FindFirstChild("PartTele") then
      r0_pr30.Block:Destroy()
   end
   _G.LockTween = false
end
BringMob = function(r0_pr289) -- proto 289
   for r4_pr289, r5_pr289 in pairs(WS.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
      -- backwards jump barrier
      if r0_pr289 == r5_pr289.Name and r5_pr289.Parent and r5_pr289:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and r5_pr289:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and 0 < r5_pr289.Humanoid.Health and r5_pr289.HumanoidRootPart.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Magnitude <= 350 then
         r5_pr289.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = BringPos
         r5_pr289.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0
         r5_pr289.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
         r5_pr289.HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 1
         r5_pr289.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
         r5_pr289.Head.CanCollide = false
         if r5_pr289.Humanoid:FindFirstChild("Animator") then
            r5_pr289.Humanoid.Animator:Destroy()
         end
         if not r5_pr289.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("Lock") then
            local r6_pr289 = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
            r6_pr289.Parent = r5_pr289.HumanoidRootPart
            r6_pr289.Name = "Lock"
            r6_pr289.MaxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 100000, 100000)
            r6_pr289.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
         end
         sethiddenproperty(plr, "SimulationRadius", math.huge)
         r5_pr289.Humanoid:ChangeState(11)
      end
   end
end
CancelTween23 = function() -- proto 178
   if plr.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("BodyVelocity") then
      plr.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("BodyVelocity"):Destroy()
   end
   if plr.Character:FindFirstChild("PartTele") then
      plr.Character:FindFirstChild("PartTele"):Destroy()
   end
   NoClip = false
   Tween23(plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
end
KillMob = function(r0_pr259, r1_pr259) -- proto 259
   pcall(function() -- proto 0
      thismob = DetectMob2(r0_pr259)
      if thismob:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and thismob.Parent and thismob:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and 0 < thismob.Humanoid.Health then
         repeat
            -- backwards jump barrier
            task.wait()
            Buso()
            EquipWeapon()
            Tween23(thismob.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 15, 0))
            BringPos = thismob.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
            BringMob(r0_pr259)
            NoClip = true
         until not thismob.Parent or not thismob:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") or thismob:FindFirstChild("Humanoid").Health <= 0 or not thismob:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or r1_pr259()
         NoClip = false
         CancelTween23()
      end
   end)
end

TweenToPosition = function(r0_pr157) -- proto 157
   local r1_pr157 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
   local r2_pr157 = not r1_pr157 or r1_pr157:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
   if not r2_pr157 then
      return
   end
   local r3_pr157 = game:GetService("TweenService")
   local r4_pr157 = r2_pr157.Position - r0_pr157.Position.Magnitude / 300
   local r5_pr157 = r3_pr157:Create(r2_pr157, TweenInfo.new(r4_pr157, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {
      .CFrame = r0_pr157
   })
   r5_pr157:Play()
   r5_pr157.Completed:Wait()
end
Skill = function(r0_pr254) -- proto 254
   local r1_pr254 = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
   r1_pr254:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[r0_pr254], false, game)
   task.wait(0.05)
   r1_pr254:SendKeyEvent(false, Enum.KeyCode[r0_pr254], false, game)
end
Click = function() -- proto 410
   local r0_pr410 = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
   r0_pr410:SendMouseButtonEvent(0, 0, 0, true, game, 1)
   task.wait(0.05)
   r0_pr410:SendMouseButtonEvent(0, 0, 0, false, game, 1)
end
FindWeapon = function(r0_pr171) -- proto 171
   local r1_pr171 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
   for r5_pr171, r6_pr171 in ipairs(r1_pr171:GetChildren()) do
   while true do
      -- backwards jump barrier
      r6_pr171:IsA("Tool")
      r0_pr171 == "Melee"
      r6_pr171.ToolTip ~= "Melee"
      r6_pr171.Name ~= "Combat"
      r0_pr171 == "Sword"
      r6_pr171.ToolTip ~= "Sword"
      if r0_pr171 == "Gun" and r6_pr171.ToolTip == "Gun" then
         return r6_pr171.Name
      end
      if r0_pr171 == "Fruit" and r6_pr171.ToolTip == "Blox Fruit" then
         return r6_pr171.Name
         return r6_pr171.Name
         return r6_pr171.Name
      end
   end
   r2_pr171 = nil
end
EquipWeapon = function(r0_pr3) -- proto 3
   if not r0_pr3 then
      return
   end
   local r1_pr3 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
   local r2_pr3 = r1_pr3:WaitForChild("Backpack"):FindFirstChild(r0_pr3)
   if r2_pr3 then
      r1_pr3.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(r2_pr3)
   end
end
AttackAllSkills = function() -- proto 379
   local r0_pr379 = FindWeapon("Melee")
   local r1_pr379 = FindWeapon("Sword")
   local r2_pr379 = FindWeapon("Fruit")
   local r3_pr379 = FindWeapon("Gun")
   if r0_pr379 then
      EquipWeapon(r0_pr379)
      Skill("Z")
      Skill("X")
      Skill("C")
      Skill("V")
      Click()
   end
   if r1_pr379 then
      EquipWeapon(r1_pr379)
      Skill("Z")
      Skill("X")
      Click()
   end
   if r2_pr379 then
      EquipWeapon(r2_pr379)
      Skill("Z")
      Skill("X")
      Skill("C")
      Skill("F")
      Click()
   end
   if r3_pr379 then
      EquipWeapon(r3_pr379)
      Skill("Z")
      Skill("X")
      Click()
   end
end

spawn(function() -- proto 66
   -- backwards jump barrier
   while wait() do
      if _G.CollectBerry then
         local r0_pr66 = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
         local r1_pr66 = r0_pr66.Character or r0_pr66.CharacterAdded:Wait():GetPivot().Position
         local r2_pr66 = game:GetService("CollectionService"):GetTagged("BerryBush")
         local r3_pr66 = math.huge
         local r4_pr66, r5_pr66 = nil, nil
         for r9_pr66, r10_pr66 in ipairs(r2_pr66) do
            -- backwards jump barrier
            for r14_pr66, r15_pr66 in pairs(r10_pr66:GetAttributes()) do
               -- backwards jump barrier
               if r3_pr66 > r10_pr66.Parent:GetPivot().Position - r1_pr66.Magnitude then
                  r5_pr66, r4_pr66, r3_pr66 = r14_pr66, r10_pr66, r16_pr66
               end
            end
         end
         if r4_pr66 and r5_pr66 then
            local r6_pr66 = r4_pr66.Parent
            local r7_pr66 = r6_pr66:GetPivot().Position
            TP1(CFrame.new(r7_pr66 + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)))
            task.wait(0.5)
            local r8_pr66 = r6_pr66:FindFirstChild(r5_pr66)
            if r8_pr66 and r8_pr66:IsA("BasePart") then
               TP1(r8_pr66.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 1, 0))
               task.wait(0.3)
               local r9_pr66 = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
               r9_pr66:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.E, false, game)
               task.wait(0.1)
               r9_pr66:SendKeyEvent(false, Enum.KeyCode.E, false, game)
            end
         else
            if _G.CollectBerryHop then
               Hop()
            end
         end
      end
   end
end)

         if _G.SelectedRod and (not r2_pr403 or r2_pr403.Name ~= _G.SelectedRod) then
            local r3_pr403 = r61_rt.Backpack:FindFirstChild(_G.SelectedRod)
            if r3_pr403 then
               r61_rt.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(r3_pr403)
               r2_pr403 = r3_pr403
            end
         end
         if r0_pr403 and r1_pr403 and r2_pr403 then
            local r3_pr403 = r65_rt(r1_pr403.Position)
            local r4_pr403, r5_pr403 = workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(Ray.new(r0_pr403.Head.Position, r1_pr403.CFrame.LookVector * r64_rt), {
               r0_pr403,
               workspace.Characters,
               workspace.Enemies
            })
            local r6_pr403 = not r5_pr403 or Vector3.new(r5_pr403.X, math.max(r5_pr403.Y, r3_pr403), r5_pr403.Z)
            local r7_pr403 = r2_pr403.GetAttribute(r2_pr403, "State")
            local r8_pr403 = r2_pr403.GetAttribute(r2_pr403, "ServerState")
            if (r7_pr403 ~= "ReeledIn" and r8_pr403 ~= "ReeledIn") or not r6_pr403 then
               if r8_pr403 == "Biting" then
                  r63_rt:InvokeServer("Catching", true)
                  task.wait(0.1)
                  r63_rt:InvokeServer("Catch", 1)
               end
            else
               r63_rt:InvokeServer("StartCasting")
               task.wait()
               r63_rt:InvokeServer("CastLineAtLocation", r6_pr403, 100, true)
            end
         end
      end
   end
end)

local r80_rt = function(r0_pr437) -- proto 437
   local r1_pr437 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
   local r2_pr437 = r1_pr437.Backpack
   for r6_pr437, r7_pr437 in pairs(r2_pr437:GetChildren()) do
      -- backwards jump barrier

spawn(function() -- proto 269
   -- backwards jump barrier
   while wait() do
      if _G.AutoPlayerHunter then
         if game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false then
            wait(0.5)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("PlayerHunter")
            break
         end
         for r3_pr269, r4_pr269 in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Characters:GetChildren()) do
            -- backwards jump barrier
            if string.find(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, r4_pr269.Name) then
               repeat
                  -- backwards jump barrier
                  wait()
                  AutoHaki()
                  EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
                  Useskill = true
                  topos(r4_pr269.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(1, 7, 3))
                  r4_pr269.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(60, 60, 60)
                  game:GetService("VirtualUser"):CaptureController()
                  game:GetService("VirtualUser"):Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672))
               until _G.AutoPlayerHunter == false or r4_pr269.Humanoid.Health <= 0
               Useskill = false
               game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AbandonQuest")
            end
         end
      end
   end
end)

spawn(function() -- proto 125
   -- backwards jump barrier
   while task.wait() do
      pcall(function() -- proto 0
         CheckQuest()
         for r3_pr125_0, r4_pr125_0 in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:GetChildren()) do
            -- backwards jump barrier
            if _G.BringMonster and ((StartBring and r4_pr125_0.Name == MonFarm) or (r4_pr125_0.Name == Mon and r4_pr125_0:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and r4_pr125_0:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and 0 < r4_pr125_0.Humanoid.Health and r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.Position - game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Magnitude <= 320)) then
               if r4_pr125_0.Name == "Factory Staff" then
                  if r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.Position - PosMon.Position.Magnitude <= 250 then
                     r4_pr125_0.Head.CanCollide = false
                     r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                     r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(60, 60, 60)
                     r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PosMon
                     if r4_pr125_0.Humanoid:FindFirstChild("Animator") then
                        r4_pr125_0.Humanoid.Animator:Destroy()
                     end
                     sethiddenproperty(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer, "SimulationRadius", math.huge)
                  end
               else
                  if (r4_pr125_0.Name == MonFarm or r4_pr125_0.Name == Mon) and r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.Position - PosMon.Position.Magnitude <= 320 then
                     r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(60, 60, 60)
                     r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PosMon
                     r4_pr125_0.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                     r4_pr125_0.Head.CanCollide = false
                     if r4_pr125_0.Humanoid:FindFirstChild("Animator") then
                        r4_pr125_0.Humanoid.Animator:Destroy()
                     end
                     sethiddenproperty(game.Players.LocalPlayer, "SimulationRadius", math.huge)
                  end
               end
            end
         end
      end)
   end
end)

end

      end
   end
